207st data
Two numbers are said to be relatively prime if they share no common positive factors other than 1. Set S contains the set of integers from 1 to 1,000, inclusive. What is the probability that a number chosen from S is relatively prime to 1,000? Answer Choices: (A) 5/7 (B) 3/5 (C) 4/7 (D) 2/5 (E) 2/7
Let's think step by step.
First, we need to find the number of positive integers from 1 to 1,000 that are relatively prime to 1,000. 

To do this, we can use Euler's totient function, which gives us the number of positive integers less than or equal to a given number that are relatively prime to it. 

For any positive integer n, the value of the totient function, denoted as φ(n), can be found using the formula:

φ(n) = n * (1 - 1/p1) * (1 - 1/p2) * ... * (1 - 1/pk)

where p1, p2, ..., pk are the distinct prime factors of n.

In this case, 1,000 = 2^3 * 5^3, so we can calculate φ(1,000) as follows:

φ(1,000) = 1,000 * (1 - 1/2) * (1 - 1/5) = 1,000 * (1/2) * (4/5) = 400

Therefore, there are 400 positive integers from 1 to 1,000 that are relatively prime to 1,000.

Next, we need to find the total number of integers in set S, which is simply 1,000.

Finally, we can calculate the probability by dividing the number of integers relatively prime to 1,000 by the total number of integers in set S:

Probability = 400/1,000 = 4/10 = 2/5

Therefore, the answer is (D) 2/5.
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is(D) 2/5.
pred_before : (D) 2/5.
pred_after : D
pred : D

During the first 7 days, the worker's total wage is 7 * 87 = 609 dollars.
During the last 7 days, the worker's total wage is 7 * 92 = 644 dollars.

Therefore, the worker's total wage for the entire fortnight is 609 + 644 = 1253 dollars.

Since the average wage for the entire fortnight is 90 dollars per day, the worker's total wage for the entire fortnight is 15 * 90 = 1350 dollars.

Therefore, the worker's wage on the 8th day is 1350 - 1253 = 97 dollars.

If 10 is subtracted from 2/3 of a number the result is equal to sum of 40 and 1/3 of the number. Find the number Answer Choices: (A) 100 (B) 160 (C) 150 (D) 210 (E) 220
Let's think step by step.
Let's assume the number is x.

According to the problem, "10 is subtracted from 2/3 of a number," we can write this as:

(2/3)x - 10

The problem also states that "the result is equal to the sum of 40 and 1/3 of the number," which can be written as:

40 + (1/3)x

Now we can set up an equation:

(2/3)x - 10 = 40 + (1/3)x

To solve this equation, we can first get rid of the fractions by multiplying every term by 3:

3 * (2/3)x - 3 * 10 = 3 * 40 + 3 * (1/3)x

2x - 30 = 120 + x

Next, we can simplify the equation by subtracting x from both sides:

2x - x - 30 = 120 + x - x

x - 30 = 120

Finally, we can solve for x by adding 30 to both sides:

x - 30 + 30 = 120 + 30

x = 150

Therefore, the number is 150.

The correct answer choice is (C) 150.
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is(C) 150

Since 10% of the chocolates are cocoa flavored, there are 10 cocoa flavored chocolates.

This means there are 100 - 10 = 90 vanilla flavored chocolates.

A merchant receives an invoice for a motor boat for $20 000 with terms 4/30, n/100. What is the highest simple interest rate at which he can afford to borrow money in order to take advantage of the discount? Answer Choices: (A) 247.67 (B) 237.67 (C) 227.67 (D) 215.67 (E) None of these
Let's think step by step.
Step 1: Calculate the discount amount.
The terms 4/30, n/100 mean that the merchant can get a 4% discount if the invoice is paid within 30 days. 
So, the discount amount is 4% of $20,000, which is 0.04 * $20,000 = $800.

Step 2: Calculate the amount the merchant needs to borrow.
The merchant needs to borrow the full amount of the invoice minus the discount amount.
So, the amount the merchant needs to borrow is $20,000 - $800 = $19,200.

Step 3: Calculate the highest simple interest rate.
The highest simple interest rate is the rate at which the merchant can afford to borrow money and still be able to pay back the loan with the discount amount.
Let's assume the interest rate is x%.

The interest on the loan is calculated as the principal (amount borrowed) multiplied by the interest rate and the time period.
In this case, the principal is $19,200, the interest rate is x%, and the time period is 30 days.

The interest on the loan is given by the formula: Interest = Principal * Rate * Time
So, the interest on the loan is $19,200 * (x/100) * (30/365) = $800.

Now, we can solve for x:
$19,200 * (x/100) * (30/365) = $800
Simplifying, we get:
x/100 = $800 / ($19,200 * (30/365))
x/100 = $800 / $1,600
x/100 = 0.5
x = 0.5 * 100
x = 50

Therefore, the highest simple interest rate at which the merchant can afford to borrow money is 50%.

Answer: None of these.
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is(E) None of these

Let's think step by step.
First, let's find the least common multiple (LCM) of 6 and 9, which is 18. This means that after 18 minutes, both machines will have produced a yo-yo.

Next, let's find out how many yo-yos each machine produces in 18 minutes. Machine A produces $\frac{18}{6} = 3$ yo-yos, and Machine B produces $\frac{18}{9} = 2$ yo-yos.

So in 18 minutes, they have produced a total of $3 + 2 = 5$ yo-yos.

To produce 10 yo-yos, they need to produce 5 more yo-yos. Since they produce 5 yo-yos in 18 minutes, they will need another 18 minutes to produce the remaining 5 yo-yos.

Therefore, the total time it takes for them to produce 10 yo-yos is $18 + 18 = \boxed{\textbf{(C) }36}$ minutes.

Ram meets Krishna at point C on the road after 10 seconds. Find the total distance between A to B. Answer Choices: (A) 700 meters (B) 1000 meters (C) 700 kilometers (D) 555 meters (E) 600 meters
Let's think step by step.
First, let's find the distance that Ram travels in 10 seconds. Since Ram's speed is 20 m/s, the distance he travels in 10 seconds is 20 m/s * 10 s = 200 meters.

Next, let's find the distance that Krishna travels in 10 seconds. Since Krishna's speed is 40 m/s, the distance he travels in 10 seconds is 40 m/s * 10 s = 400 meters.

Since Ram and Krishna meet at point C, the total distance between A and B is the sum of the distances they traveled to reach point C. Therefore, the total distance between A and B is 200 meters + 400 meters = 600 meters.

Let's think step by step.
Step 1: We know that the median income is $3000. This means that there are an equal number of family members earning less than $3000 and an equal number of family members earning more than $3000.

Step 2: Let's assume that there are $n$ family members earning less than $3000 and $n$ family members earning more than $3000.

Step 3: The total income of the family is $9000. Since there are $n$ family members earning less than $3000, their total income is $3000n$. Similarly, the total income of the family members earning more than $3000 is $3000n$.

Step 4: Adding the two total incomes together, we get $3000n + 3000n = 9000$. Simplifying, we have $6000n = 9000$.

Step 5: Dividing both sides of the equation by 6000, we find that $n = \frac{9000}{6000} = \frac{3}{2}$. Since $n$ represents the number of family members, it cannot be a fraction. Therefore, there must be a whole number of family members earning less than $3000 and a whole number of family members earning more than $3000.

Step 6: The only whole number that satisfies this condition is $n = 1$. This means that there is 1 family member earning less than $3000 and 1 family member earning more than $3000.

Step 7: Adding these two family members together, we find that there are $1 + 1 = 2$ family members in total.

Step 8: Therefore, the answer is $\boxed{\text{(A) } 2}$.
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is$\boxed{\text{(A) } 2}$.
pred_before : $\boxed{\text{(A) } 2}$.
pred_after : A
pred : A
GT : B

A rectangular parking space is marked out by painting three of its sides. If the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, and the sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, then what is the area of the parking space in square feet? Answer Choices: (A) 46 (B) 81 (C) 126 (D) 252 (E) None
Let's think step by step.
Let's call the length of the painted side $x$ and the width of the parking space $y$. We know that the length of the unpainted side is 9 feet, so $y = 9$. 

The sum of the lengths of the painted sides is 37 feet, so $2x + y = 37$. Substituting $y = 9$, we get $2x + 9 = 37$. Solving for $x$, we find that $x = 14$. 

The area of a rectangle is given by the formula $A = \text{length} \times \text{width}$. Substituting $x = 14$ and $y = 9$, we get $A = 14 \times 9 = 126$. 

Therefore, the area of the parking space is $\boxed{\textbf{(C) }126}$ square feet.

If that projection were to come true, the population two years from now would be exactly double the population of one year ago. Which of the following is closest to the percent population increase in Boomtown over the last year? Answer Choices: (A) 20% (B) 40% (C) 50% (D) 65% (E) 75%
Let's think step by step.
Let's assume the population of Boomtown one year ago was x.

According to the given information, the population two years from now would be exactly double the population of one year ago. So, the population two years from now would be 2x.

We are also given that the city's population is expected to increase by 10% per year over the next two years. This means that the population one year from now would be x + 0.1x = 1.1x.

Now, we can calculate the percent population increase over the last year by finding the difference between the population one year from now and the population one year ago, and then expressing it as a percentage of the population one year ago.

Percent population increase = ((Population one year from now - Population one year ago) / Population one year ago) * 100
= ((1.1x - x) / x) * 100
= (0.1x / x) * 100
= 10%

Therefore, the percent population increase in Boomtown over the last year is 10%.

The closest answer choice to 10% is (A) 20%.

Answer Choices: (A) $45,000 (B) $50,000 (C) $54,000 (D) $59,000 (E) $62,000
Let's think step by step.
First, let's set up the formula for compound interest: 

A = P(1 + r/n)^(nt)

Where:
A = the final amount (including principal and interest)
P = the principal amount (the initial investment)
r = the annual interest rate (as a decimal)
n = the number of times that interest is compounded per year
t = the number of years

In this case, we know that:
A = $54,080
r = 8% = 0.08
n = 2 (compounded semi-annually)
t = 1 year

So the formula becomes:
$54,080 = P(1 + 0.08/2)^(2*1)

Simplifying the equation:
$54,080 = P(1.04)^2

$54,080 = P(1.0816)

Now, divide both sides of the equation by 1.0816 to solve for P:
P = $54,080 / 1.0816

P ≈ $50,000

Therefore, the amount of money that Charles originally invested is approximately $50,000. The correct answer choice is (B) $50,000.

A cow is tethered in the middle of a field with a 14 feet long rope. If the cow grazes 10 sq.ft. per day, then approximately what time will be taken by the cow to graze the whole field? Answer Choices: (A) 51 days (B) 61 days (C) 71 days (D) 81 days (E) 91 days
Let's think step by step.
First, let's find the area of the field. Since the field is circular and the rope is the radius, the area of the field is given by the formula A = πr^2, where r is the length of the rope. Plugging in the given value, we have A = π(14/2)^2 = 49π sq.ft.

Next, let's find the area the cow grazes in one day. The cow grazes 10 sq.ft. per day, so in 1 day, it grazes an area of 10 sq.ft.

To find the number of days it takes for the cow to graze the whole field, we divide the total area of the field by the area grazed in one day. So, the number of days is 49π sq.ft. / 10 sq.ft. = 4.9π.

Since we are looking for an approximate answer, we can use the approximation π ≈ 3.14. So, the number of days is approximately 4.9 * 3.14 = 15.386.

Rounding up to the nearest whole number, the cow will take approximately 16 days to graze the whole field.

However, none of the answer choices are close to 16 days. Let's check our calculations.

If we use the approximation π ≈ 3.14, the number of days is 49 * 3.14 / 10 = 15.386.

Rounding up to the nearest whole number, the cow will take approximately 16 days to graze the whole field.

He divides the amount in such a way that if their shares are invested at compound interest at 4% p.a. they will receive equal amount on attaining the age of 26 years. Find Mohan's share. Answer Choices: (A) 2400 (B) 2500 (C) 2600 (D) 2700 (E) None of these
Let's think step by step.
Step 1: Let's assume that Mohan's share is x rupees. So, Sohan's share will be (5100 - x) rupees.

Step 2: Now, let's calculate the amount that Mohan will receive on attaining the age of 26 years. The compound interest formula is given by:

A = P(1 + r/n)^(nt)

Where:
A = the final amount
P = the principal amount
r = the annual interest rate (in decimal form)
n = the number of times that interest is compounded per year
t = the number of years

In this case, Mohan's share (x rupees) will be invested for 3 years (from the age of 23 to 26) at an interest rate of 4% per annum. So, the formula becomes:

A1 = x(1 + 0.04/1)^(1*3)
A1 = x(1.04)^3

Step 3: Now, let's calculate the amount that Sohan will receive on attaining the age of 26 years. Sohan's share (5100 - x rupees) will also be invested for 3 years (from the age of 24 to 26) at an interest rate of 4% per annum. So, the formula becomes:

A2 = (5100 - x)(1 + 0.04/1)^(1*2)
A2 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2

Step 4: According to the given condition, Mohan and Sohan will receive equal amounts on attaining the age of 26 years. So, we can equate A1 and A2:

x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2

Step 5: Simplifying the equation:

x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2
x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2
x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2
x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2
x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2
x(1.04)^3 = (5100 - x)(1.04)^2

Let's think step by step.
Let's assume that the coin-diver brought x copper coins and y brass coins.

According to the given information, for each copper coin, the coin-diver gets 20 cents, and for each brass coin, she gets 25 cents.

So, the total amount of money she gets from the copper coins is 20x cents, and the total amount of money she gets from the brass coins is 25y cents.

We are also given that after one dive, she got $3.40, which is equal to 340 cents.

Therefore, we can write the equation: 20x + 25y = 340.

Now, we need to find the minimum number of copper coins that she brought. To do that, we can start by assuming that she brought the maximum number of brass coins possible, which is 13 (since 25 multiplied by 13 is 325, which is less than 340).

If she brought 13 brass coins, then the equation becomes: 20x + 25(13) = 340.
Simplifying this equation, we get: 20x + 325 = 340.
Subtracting 325 from both sides, we get: 20x = 15.
Dividing both sides by 20, we get: x = 0.75.

Since the number of coins must be a whole number, we can conclude that she did not bring any copper coins (x = 0).

Therefore, the minimum number of copper coins that she brought is 0.

Simple Interest - Compound Interest = 72

Let's think step by step.
First, we need to find the total number of parts in the mixture. Since the ratio of rice, wheat, and corn is 2:3:5, the total number of parts is $2+3+5=10$.

Next, we need to find the weight of each part. Since the bag contains 3 pounds of rice, and rice is 2 parts out of 10, each part weighs $\frac{3}{2}$ pounds.

Finally, we need to find the weight of the corn. Since corn is 5 parts out of 10, the weight of the corn is $\frac{5}{10} \cdot \frac{3}{2} = \frac{15}{20} = \frac{3}{4}$ pounds.

Therefore, the bag contains $\boxed{\text{(E) None of the above}}$ pounds of corn.

Answer Choices: (A) 12 am on the next day (B) 5 am on the next day (C) 5 pm on the next day (D) 2 pm on the next day (E) None of these
Let's think step by step.
First, let's find out the time difference between the two trains. Train A leaves at 11 am and Train B leaves at 2 pm, so the time difference is 3 hours.

Now, let's calculate the distance covered by Train A in these 3 hours. Since Train A is running at a speed of 40 kmph, it covers a distance of 40 kmph * 3 hours = 120 km.

Now, let's find out how long it takes for Train B to cover this distance. Since Train B is running at a speed of 72 kmph, it takes Train B 120 km / 72 kmph = 1.67 hours to cover this distance.

Therefore, the two trains will meet each other 1.67 hours after Train B starts its journey, which is at 2 pm. Adding this time to 2 pm, we get 3:40 pm.

However, we need to consider the time difference between the two trains. Since Train A started 3 hours earlier, we need to subtract 3 hours from 3:40 pm.

Therefore, the two trains will meet each other at 12:40 pm.

The correct answer is (E) None of these, as none of the answer choices match the calculated time.

253st data
The ratio of the volumes of a cube to that of the sphere which will fit inside the cube is? Answer Choices: (A) 2: π (B) 7:2 (C) 8:2 (D) 6: π (E) 8:3
Let's think step by step.
First, let's find the volume of the cube. Since all sides of a cube are equal, let's assume the side length of the cube is $s$. Therefore, the volume of the cube is $s^3$.

Next, let's find the volume of the sphere. The volume of a sphere is given by the formula $\frac{4}{3}\pi r^3$, where $r$ is the radius of the sphere. Since the sphere fits inside the cube, the diameter of the sphere is equal to the side length of the cube. Therefore, the radius of the sphere is $\frac{s}{2}$. Substituting this value into the formula for the volume of the sphere, we get $\frac{4}{3}\pi \left(\frac{s}{2}\right)^3 = \frac{4}{3}\pi \cdot \frac{s^3}{8} = \frac{\pi s^3}{6}$.

Finally, let's find the ratio of the volumes of the cube to the sphere. Dividing the volume of the cube by the volume of the sphere, we get $\frac{s^3}{\frac{\pi s^3}{6}} = \frac{6}{\pi}$. Therefore, the ratio of the volumes of the cube to the sphere is $\boxed{\textbf{(D) }6:\pi}$.
Therefore, among A through E, the answer is$\boxed{\textbf{(D) }6:\pi}$.
